font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">NOBODY --&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">AS BART WAS CATEGORY 5.ON THE SAFFIR\nSIMPSON'S SCALE, &nbsp;WITH WINDS OF 262 KILOMETERS PER HOUR.</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bart would soon kill\nmore than 30 people and&nbsp; destroy more\nthan 80000 homes in Japan and cause 4 billion USD in damages.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The previous\nrecord was a category 5 typhoon Vera on Sept 26th 1959 -- less powerful than\nBart.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Punch into Google\nsearch-- <span style=\"color: red;\"><b>SUPER TYPHOON BART, THE PERFECT STORM- VADAKAYIL</b></span>,&nbsp; to see a blow by blow account of what\ntranspired 13 years ago.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-A3ZZf9iZ7_g/UDoyhhIBMGI/AAAAAAAAQDY/yVyRxXsqfA0/s1600/ghhj.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"312\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-A3ZZf9iZ7_g/UDoyhhIBMGI/AAAAAAAAQDY/yVyRxXsqfA0/s400/ghhj.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Year 2012 is a El Nino\nyear.&nbsp; West Pacific is gonna be battered\nby typhoons. Australia will have droughts and forest fires.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Correspondingly the\nhurricanes in the S Atlantic , Carriebean&nbsp;\nbearing towards the East coast of USA will be&nbsp; less, due to wind shear tearing them up.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">During El Nino, the\nwaters in the central and eastern Pacific are warmer than normal, and the\neffects on global weather can be drastic and far-reaching.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">You get to see\n\"Super Typhoons\" during El Nino years.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The El Nino starts\nafter a pool of hot seawater almost the size of USA, ( more than 15 million\nsquare kms ) appears off the west coast of the Americas. &nbsp;The ocean would heat\nup right around Christmas time, so fishermen call the phenomenon El Ni\u00f1o, for\nthe Christ Child.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Usually, the wind blows\nstrongly from east to west along the equator in the Pacific. This actually\npiles up water (about half a meter's worth) in the western part of the Pacific.\nIn the eastern part, deeper water (which is colder than the sun-warmed surface\nwater) gets pulled up from below to replace the water pushed west. So, the\nnormal situation is warm water (about 30 C) in the west, cold (about 22 C) in\nthe east.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In an El Ni\u00f1o, the\nwinds pushing that water around get weaker. As a result, some of the warm water\npiled up in the west slumps back down to the east, and not as much cold water\ngets pulled up from below. Both these tend to make the water in the eastern\nPacific warmer, which is one of the hallmarks of an El Ni\u00f1o.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">But it doesn't stop\nthere. The warmer ocean then affects the winds--it makes the winds weaker! So\nif the winds get weaker, then the ocean gets warmer, which makes the winds get\nweaker, which makes the ocean get warmer ... this is called a positive\nfeedback, and is what makes an El Ni\u00f1o grow.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The ocean has a wave\ncalled a Rossby wave that is quite unlike the waves you see when you visit the\nbeach. It's more like a distant cousin to a tidal wave. The difference is that\na tidal wave goes very quickly, with all the water moving pretty much in the\nsame direction. In a Rossby wave, the upper part of the ocean, say the top 100\nmeters or so, will be leisurely sliding one way, while the lower part, starting\nat 100 meters and going on down, will be slowly moving the other way.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">After a while they\nswitch directions. Everything happens very slowly and inside the ocean, and you\ncan't even see them on the surface. These things are so slow, they can take\nmonths or years to cross the oceans. If you had the patience to sit there while\none was going by, you'd hardly notice it; the water would be moving only\n1/100th of walking speed. But they are large, hundreds or thousands of\nkilometers in length (not height! Remember, you can hardly see them on the\nsurface), so they can have an effect on things.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Another wave you rarely\nhear about is called a Kelvin wave, and it has some characteristics in common\nwith Rossby waves, but is somewhat faster and can only exist close to the\nequator (say, within about 5 degrees of latitude around the equator). El Ninos\noften start with a Kelvin wave propagating from the western Pacific over\ntowards South America.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When an El Ni\u00f1o gets\ngoing in the middle or eastern part of the Pacific, it creates Rossby waves\nthat drift slowly towards southeast Asia. After several months of travelling,\nthey finally get near the coast and reflect back. The changes in interior ocean\ntemperature that these waves carry with it \"cancel out\" the original\ntemperature changes that made the El Ni\u00f1o in the first place. A strong El Ni\u00f1o\ncan last a year or more before conditions return to normal. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Punch into google\nsearch&nbsp;<b><span style=\"color: red;\"> EL NINO, A MARINERS OVER VIEW -\nVADAKAYIL</span></b>,&nbsp; to check out my experiences\nwith El Nino.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\">My thoughts are with the poor sailors who lose their lives every year in stormy seas -- never to be talked about or remembered--&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\">-- while if a rich banker in a passenger airplane of the first class section spills beer on himself, as he was inebriated--&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\">--nay--&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\">-- due to an air pocket, &nbsp;the event becomes BREAKING news in Time and Newsweek.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-CjLjlnjvHc4/UDoyGLWZdJI/AAAAAAAAQDQ/jDnQsuOzJoM/s1600/PAA7140036.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; None of the said letters/averments was denied or\ndisputed or controverted by anyone including yourself. 2.<o:p></o:p></span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\">SK Srivastava applied\nand obtained copies of the files and papers from the ministry of finance\ncertified by the appropriate authority as the true copies of the said files and\npapers on 25.6.2008 under the RTI Act 2005. As evident from the traces of\ncrime which could not be erased, this was how the files/records have been\nfabricated:<o:p></o:p></span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; This is because the filing procedure of the government\nwould not allow easy tampering with the files. Any tampering can be discovered\nas explaining hereunder:<o:p></o:p></span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\">\ue000<o:p></o:p></span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue;\">The filing procedures\nrequire entry into the file register of the concerned section of the\ndepartment, the moment a file is opened and a separate and distinct new number\nis given to each file. So file referred to File 113/06 bears the number 113/06\nand File 36/06 bears the number 36/06.<o:p></o:p></span></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; Line dancers are not\nin physical contact with each other.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I have seen spontaneous line dances in\nSydney and Melbourne-NOT premeditated like our Kolaveri Di .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is east to find\nout when the genders even out.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\nNot many people know that the inspiration for this song was the Texas chainsaw massacre. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "2", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7136296228620611256/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "1238462202474487427", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-08-21T09:25:00+05:30", "updated": "2018-06-27T05:29:56+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTMwMDU3NTk2OTg3Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/08/instructions-for-overflow-prevention-on.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/1238462202474487427", "title": "", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Wfsjdh1ov2E/UDMGnUFWfpI/AAAAAAAAPys/pNajW6Kx8oY/s1600/AAA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"208\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Wfsjdh1ov2E/UDMGnUFWfpI/AAAAAAAAPys/pNajW6Kx8oY/s320/AAA.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<b><span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">INSTRUCTIONS FOR OVERFLOW PREVENTION ON CHEMICAL\nTANKERS</span>-&nbsp; CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</span><span style=\"font-size: xx-small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">1)ON XXXX ANY OVERFLOW / POLLUTION IS DEEMED AS PERSONNEL\nERROR. &nbsp;NO EXCUSE HOLDS WATER WITH CAPT VADAKAYIL.\nTHIS IS ONE CAPTAIN AT WHOM YOU CANT THROW SILLY EXCUSES LIKE AIR LOCK. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">2)AN OIL TANKER MAN IS A MISFIT ON A CHEMICAL TANKER AS FLUID\nMECHANICS PRINCIPLES DIFFER. ON AN OIL TANKER YOU PREVENT OVERFLOW BY OPENING\nANOTHER EMPTY TANK VALVE.&nbsp; HERE YOU SHUT\nTHE&nbsp; FULL TANK VALVE. &nbsp;FOR ON OIL TANKERS THE TANKS ARE CONNECTED AT\nTHE BOTTOM WHILE ON CHEMICAL TANKERS THE LINES ARE CONNECTED ON TOP.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">3)SO ON A ULCC IF THE LOADING RATE IS 20000 TOMS PER HOUR IT\nDOES NOT MEAN YOU WILL NEED TO TOP UP ANY TANK AT THIS FANTASTIC RATE. YOU\nREDUCE THE SHIPS TANK LOADING RATE TO SUIT YOUR OWN STANDARD OF COMFORT BY\nBLEEDING OFF TO ANOTHER TANK . THIS COULD BE EVEN NEGATIVE RATE IN CASE YOU WANT\nTO BUY TIME DUE TO SOME UNFORSEEN EMERGENCY ( LIKE NATURE\u2019S CALL )<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">4) ON CHEMICAL TANKERS YOU CANNOT BUY A NEGATIVE RATE. THIS\nMEANS YOU MUST BE LOADING THE NEXT TANK WELL BEFORE YOU SHUT A TOPPED UP TANK.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">5)THE LAST TANK MUST BE TOPPED UP BY REDUCING THE SHORE\nLOADING RATE. AND NEVER TRY TO LOAD LAST TANK TO MORE THAN 95 PERCENT.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">6)ORDERS ON WALKIE TALKIE MUST BE SHORT AND CRISP LIKE BRIDGE\nHELM ORDERS. YOU DON\u2019T GIVE A STRING OF HELM AND TELEGRAPH ORDERS ON THE BRIDGE\n, RIGHT?<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">7)KEEP SPARE WALKIE TALKIE BATTERIES AT STRATEGIC PLACES.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">8)REMEMBER PV VENT IS ALSO PART OF LOADING SYSTEM. VENTS CAN\nGET FROZEN ESPECIALLY WITH HIGH MP CARGO VAPOUR.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">9)KEEP STEAM HOSES READY FOR HIGH MELTING POINT CARGOES IN\nPIPELINES. &nbsp;HOT WATER AT 96 DEG C ON\nWRAPPED HESSIAN IS MORE EFFECTIVE THAN STEAM, WHICH IS TOO LOCAL<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">10)NEVER ALLOW STATIC HIGH MP CARGO INSIDE COLD PIPELINES.\nDON\u2019T TRY TO FIGHT GRAVITY WHEN BLOWING THROUGH. THE AIR ALWAYS FINDS THE\nHIGHEST POINT AND WILL SKIM ON TOP OF CARGO. THINK INTELLIGENTLY. THE PIPELINES\nARE 3D. LIQUIDS ALWAYS FIND LOWEST LEVEL. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">11) USE SINGLE STATION TO PREVENT OVERFLOW, NO RUNNING FROM\nONE TANK TO OTHER. THIS IS IMPORTANT WHEN YOU DISCHG INTO LORRIES. SIPHONING\nEFFECT CONTINUES EVEN IF PUMP IS STOPPED.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">12)PACE YOURSELF LIKE A MARATHON RUNNER. FATIGUE IS TOO LAME\nAN EXCUSE. I HATE TO SEE MY CHIEF OFFICER SLEEPING IN CCR AND HALLUCINATING\nTHAT HE IS \u201cJOAN OF ARC\u201d ----LIKE MUNGERILAL OF DOORDASHAN FAME.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">13)LASHING VAVES MUST BE DONE INTELLIGENTLY , NOT LIKE A MORON.\nYOU NORMALLY LASH VALVES YOU DO NOT WANT ITS STATUS TO BE ALTERED . THIS COULD\nMEAN A THAT A VALVE IS LASHED OPEN. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">14)TOPPING IS DONE BY SHUTTING A SINGLE VALVE. &nbsp;EXAMPLE--DO NOT HAVE THE PUMP DELIVERY AND\nDROP BOTH OPEN.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">15)EMERGENCY STOP WRITTEN PROCEDURES MUST BE AVAILABLE IN\nCCR. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">16)DURING STILL AIR CONDITIONS THE PV CONE MUST LIFT TO SHOOT\nGASES SKY HIGH AT GREATER THAN FLAME EXIT VELOCITY. &nbsp;FOR NON FLAMMABLE, NON TOXIC AND NON\nBIOACCUMULATIVE CARGOES , YOU CAN LET OUT THE HAS VIA FLAME ARRESTOR FITTED\nPURGE PIPE OR VACUUM SIDE PV VENT, IF THERE ARE NO STILL AIR CONDITIONS.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">17)TRY OUT UTI WELL IN ADVANCE. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">18)SHUT ALL DRAINS . HIGHLIGHT DRAIN COCKS.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">19)CONSTANT CHIT CHAT OF VHF TO ENSURE COMMUNICATION CHANNEL\nIS OPEN. THIS WAY EVEN IF A PIRATE IS ENGAGED IN PLAYING RUSSIAN ROULETTE WITH\nYOUR DECK HAND YOU WILL&nbsp; SUSPECT\nSOMETHING IS WRONG. ( THIS IS A TRUE NIGERIAN STORY ).&nbsp; HAVE AN EXIT CHANNEL KNOWN TO ALL IN CASE\nSOME MONKEY TRIES TO JAM YOUR CHANNEL WHILE TOPPING UP.&nbsp; WHEN CHIEF OFFICER&nbsp; ENTERS A TANK WITH A SURVEYOR&nbsp; DO NOT USE LOW POWER VHF CHANNELS LIKE 15 OR\n17 UNLESS HE HAS TAKEN IT TO DO INTERNAL TANK COMMUNICATIONS!!<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">20)CONSULT TRIM TABLES FOR TOPPING ULLAGE .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">21)DO NOT LOAD ANY TANK GREATER THAN 97 PERCENT UNLESS MASTER\nAPPROVES. THE OVERFLOW ALARM AT 98% IS NOT TO BE ACTIVATED WHILE LOADING. &nbsp; IF THE LOADING IS DONE BY SCREW PUMPS OR RECIPROCATING PISTON &nbsp;PUMPS AGAINST WHICH YOU CANNOT SHUT THE SHIP'S VALVE , &nbsp;CHIEF OFFICER MUST TAKE THIS IN WRITING AT THE PRE-LOADING MEETING.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">22)HIGH MP CARGOES WHICH ARE DANGEROUS TO BLOW LIKE PHENOL\nAND HMD, USE STEAM TRACING. &nbsp;PHENOL\nVAPOUR FALLS AS DEADLY POISON WHITE SNOW FLAKES!! &nbsp;TWO SQUARE INCHES ON YOUR SKIN AND YOU ARE\nDEAD.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">23)TANKS ALREADY TOPPED UP, MARK ON CCR BOARD. A DUPLICATE\nBOARD MUST BE AVAILABLE ON DECK IF TOO MANY THINGS ARE HAPPENING.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">24)TROOP IN TROOP OUT VIA CCR. &nbsp;YOU DO NOT NEED AN ALOMETER TO DECLARE A CREW\nMEMBER INEBRIATED &nbsp;AND&nbsp; UNFIT.&nbsp;\nIT IS YOUR JUDGEMENT AND YOUR WORD. YOU ARE THE CHIEF /DUTY -OFFICER. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">25)MASTER MONITORS ON WALKI E TALKIE. &nbsp;BASICALLY HE IS NOT GIVING ATTENTION UNLESS HE\nNOTICES CHANGE OF VOICE TONE IN PANIC. SO DO NOT GO INTO THE SHRILL MODE\nUNNECESSARILY. &nbsp;ANYBODY CONSTANTLY DOING\nTHIS WITHOUT REASON &nbsp;&nbsp;WILL NOT BE A\nCUSTODIAN OF A WALKIE TALKIE ANY MORE.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\nCALL A VALVE DUTY HAND BY NAME .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">26)DOUBLE CHECK LINES PRIOR CARGO COMMENCEMENT. THIS&nbsp; MUST BE DONE BY 2 INDEPENDENT SOULS.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">27)WHEN CARGO STARTS USE ONLY ONE TANK. &nbsp;LISTEN TO THE DYNAMIC FLOW AT MANIFOLD . DO\nNOT LOOK ONLY AT THE PRESSURE GAUGE . PRESSURE GAUGE CAN REGISTER STATIC\nPRESSURE. (FLOW METER REGISTERS DYNAMIC.)<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">28)DO NOT LOAD CARGOES LIKE ISOMERATE OF 0.62 SG TO 97\nPERCENT. THE COEFFICIENT OF EXP MUST BE CONSIDERED AND THE AMBIENT TEMP ON SEA\nPASSAGE ENROUTE TO NEXT PORT.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">29)IF SHORE SUDDENLY STOPS , DRAIN LINES IMMEDIATELY INTO\nTANK. &nbsp;WITH SOME HIGH MP CARGOES AT A\nFREEZING PORT.&nbsp; &nbsp;IT IS CHEAPER AND &nbsp;EASIER TO CUT A PIPELINE AND THROW IT AWAY\nTHAN TO ATTEMPT TO MELT THE CONTENTS . FAILURE TO DO THIS WILL CAUSE VSL TO GO\nOFFHIRE . FIGURE OUT ALL THIS WELL IN ADVANCE. <span style=\"color: red;\">THIS IS\nTHE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN A CHEMICAL MAN AND AN OILMAN.&nbsp; WE PONDER IN ADVANCE AND NOT AFTER &nbsp;S#IT &nbsp;HAS HIT THE FAN.&nbsp; &nbsp;WE\nPREVENT AND NOT CURE</span>.&nbsp; &nbsp;A CHEMICAL MAN WEARS A SAFETY HARNESS NOT A\nLIFE JACKET WHEN TAKING IN THE GANGWAY.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">30)OPEN MANIFOLD VALVE A FEW SECONDS PRIOR START. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">31)IF RAIN WATER ACCUMULATION ON DECK IS OILY EITHER SIPHON\nIT OFF OR DRAIN IT INTO THE DRAIN TANK.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">32)BALLAST 2 OFFSET ULLAGE TANKS. THAT WAY YOU DO NOT HAVE\nTANK RUPTURE IF FIRST ONE OVERFLOWS.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">33) ALL CREW MEMBERS MUST BE FAMILIAR WITH FRAMO EMERGENCY\nSTOP BUTTON.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">34)REMEMBER MANIFOLD TRAY VOLUME IS CALCULATED ON EVEN KEEL,\nNOT ON WEDGE FORMULA AT THE CURRENT STERN TRIM.<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></span>\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">35)&nbsp; WHEN DISCHARGING HIGH MELTING POINT CARGOES\nIN FREEZING WEATHER, BE AWARE THAT PIPELINE INNER DIAMETERS COULD VARY DUE TO\nFREEZING OF CARGO, AND THIS AFFECTS THE FLOW RATE. SUDDEN DISLODGING OF SAY A\nCHUNK OF PALM OIL STEARIC ACID, COULD BLOCK A PIPELINE BEND .&nbsp;&nbsp; PRIOR DISCHARGE RUN DOWN ALL TANKS BELOW 93%\nAND THEN PUT THE HIGH LEVEL (95%) AND OVERFLOW ( 98%) ALARMS ON.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\">&nbsp;THIS OPERATION MUST BE DONE BY CHIEF OFFICER. MAKE SURE THE TRIM IS NOT TOO\nHIGH WHEN YOU DO THIS. &nbsp;CHEMICAL TANKER TANKS ARE MORE IN NUMBER AND SOME ARE SMALL, WITH LESSER CAPACITY PUMPS, WITH ONLY ONE VENT USUALLY RIGHT AFT FITTED INTO THE TANK DOME. &nbsp; NO PRIZES FOR OVERFLOWING CARGO WHILE DISCHARGING. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-09o-nK8MBnI/UDMIb-h_LwI/AAAAAAAAPy0/B09yKA4Z2Bk/s1600/PC040084.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">AS LONG AS YOU\nUNDERSTAND THAT WHEN SEVERAL CHOICES ARE AVAILABLE DUE TO INTERNAL LOOPING AT\nMANIFOLD&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ( WITH Y / U PIECES AND CARGO\nHOSES) ,&nbsp; LIQUID TAKES ALWAYS THE PATH OF\nLEAST RESISTANCE AND TENDS TO GO DOWN BY GRAVITY&nbsp; , YOU WILL NOT SCREW IT UP.&nbsp; BE CAREFUL , AS SOMETIMES YOU DISCHARGE ON\nSHORE SIDE AS WELL AS SEA SIDE INTO BARGES&nbsp;\nSIMULTANEOUSLY.</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><span style=\"font-size: xx-small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><br /></span></span></span>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 200%;\"><span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\">36)THINK NEGATIVE LIKE THE JAPANESE. &nbsp;&nbsp;POLLUTION IS ONE AREA WHERE THINKING POSITIVE\nIS NOT AN ASSET. &nbsp;FOR IF YOU OVERFLOW THE\nCOMPANY COULD GET WIPED OUT. &nbsp;&nbsp;THE P AND I\nCOVER IS ONE BILLION USD FOR A GOOD REASON.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
